<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шевелиться.html>шевели́ться</a> (2852)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шевелить.html>шевели́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ševelítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шевелиться.html>шевели́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ševelítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пошевелиться.html>пошевели́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шевельнуться.html>шевельну́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to move, to stir, to budge
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сиде́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шевелиться.html>шевеля́сь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sidétʹ ne <b>ševeljásʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to sit without stirring</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шевелиться.html>шевели́сь</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ševelísʹ</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">look lively/slippy!; get a move on!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to awaken, to show signs of life</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">thoughts, feelings, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> to appear</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шевелить.html>шевели́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ševelítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">stir, move</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двигаться.html>дви́гаться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dvígatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">awaken</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробуждаться.html>пробужда́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">probuždátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">appear</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возникать.html>возника́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">voznikátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:появляться.html>появля́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pojavljátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шевельнуться.html>шевельну́ться</a> (7515)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шевельнуть.html>шевельну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ševelʹnútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шевельнуться.html>шевельну́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ševelʹnútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шевелиться.html>шевели́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stir, to move
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шевельнуться.html>шевельну́лся</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on ne <b>ševelʹnúlsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he never stirred; he did not even budge</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to awaken, to show signs of life</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">thoughts, feelings, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> to appear</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шевельнуть.html>шевельну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ševelʹnútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">move, stir</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пошевельну́ться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poševelʹnútʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">awaken</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробудиться.html>пробуди́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">probudítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">appear</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возникнуть.html>возни́кнуть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vozníknutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:появиться.html>появи́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pojavítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">chevelure</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***шелк.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шелк.html>шёлк</a> (8382)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">шьлкъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šĭlkŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Germanic languages">Germanic</a></span> language. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">silki</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шелк.html>шёлк</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šolk</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шелк.html>шёлка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шелк.html>шелка́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шелковый.html>шелко́в</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шелковый.html>шёлковый</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>silk (fiber and fabric)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> clothes made of silk
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:всегда.html>всегда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шелк.html>шелка́х</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кичиться.html>кичи́лась</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́тим</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oná vsegdá xodíla v <b>šelkáx</b> i kičílasʹ étim</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">She always showed off wearing silk (clothes).</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>something soft and pleasant for touching
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шелк.html>Шёлк</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>воло́с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нежный.html>не́жно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лечь.html>лёг</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:плечо.html>пле́чи</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Šólk</b> jejó volós néžno ljóg mne na pléči.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The silk of her hair gently lay down on my shoulders.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шелковистый.html>шелкови́стый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">šelkovístyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шелковица.html>шелкови́ца</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">šelkovíca</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:великий.html>вели́кий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шелковый.html>шёлковый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>путь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">Velíkij šólkovyj putʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:долг.html>долга́х</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шелк.html>шелка́х</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">v dolgáx kak v šelkáx</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<i>phrase: owing money to everybody, lit.: (clad) in debts like in silk (clothes)</i>)</li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:брюхо.html>брю́хе</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шелк.html>шёлк</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:брюхо.html>брю́хе</a> - <a href = vnd.unilang:щелк.html>щёлк</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">na brjúxe šólk, a v brjúxe - ščólk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<i>phrase: all hat and no cattle, lit.: belly (wrapped) in silk, and in the belly - just a click</i>)</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шелохнуться.html>шелохну́ться</a> (12509)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">шелохну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šeloxnútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шелохнуться.html>шелохну́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šeloxnútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to stir, to move
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стоя́ть</a> - <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шелохнуться.html>шелохну́ться</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">stojátʹ - ne <b>šeloxnútʹsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to stand stock-still</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:листок.html>листо́к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шелохнуться.html>шелохнётся</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">listók ne <b>šeloxnjótsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">not a leaf is stirring</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">шелохну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šeloxnútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***шельма.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шельма.html>ше́льма</a> (22909)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">schelme</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">szelma</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шельма.html>ше́льма</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šélʹma</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шельма.html>ше́льмы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шельма.html>ше́льмы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шельма.html>ше́льм</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rascal, rogue, scoundrel</li></ol>

***шепнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шепнуть.html>шепну́ть</a> (4043)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шепнуть.html>шепну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šepnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шептать.html>шепта́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to whisper</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>A rare and awkward past passive participle <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шепнуть.html>шёпнутый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šópnutyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is occasionally found.
</p>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">шёпотом</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">šópotom</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***шептать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шептать.html>шепта́ть</a> (3503)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*šьpъtati</i>, of onomatopoeic origin.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шептать.html>шепта́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šeptátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прошептать.html>прошепта́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шепнуть.html>шепну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to whisper (to talk in a quiet voice)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;;">
